<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;2.02. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Results of Operations and Financial Condition.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">On April&#160;23, 2020, Domino&#8217;s Pizza, Inc. issued a press release announcing financial results for the first quarter ended March&#160;22, 2020. A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit 99.1. The information in this Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and the Exhibit attached hereto are being furnished pursuant to Item 2.02 of Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">8-K</span> and therefore shall not be deemed filed for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

<td style="width:10%;vertical-align:top;white-space:nowrap;">Item&#160;7.01. </td>
<td style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0pt;margin-top:0pt;">Regulation FD Disclosure.</td> </tr> </table> <p style="font-family:Times New Roman;text-align:left;font-size:10pt;margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:6pt">The information included in the press release referred to above is also incorporated herein. The information in this Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;8-K</span>&#160;and the Exhibit attached hereto are being furnished pursuant to Item 7.01 of Form<span style="white-space:nowrap">&#160;8-K</span>&#160;and therefore shall not be deemed filed for purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934. </p> <p style="margin-bottom:0px;margin-top:18pt"></p>

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

</TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="middle"><FONT STYLE="font-size:11pt"><B>For Immediate Release</B></FONT></TD>
<TD VALIGN="bottom">&nbsp;&nbsp;</TD>
<TD VALIGN="middle" ALIGN="right"> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Contact: Tim McIntyre, Executive Vice President,</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Communication, Investor Relations and Legislative Affairs</B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:1pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>(734) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">930-3563</FONT></B></P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B><U>Domino&#146;s Pizza <SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> Announces First Quarter 2020 Financial Results and
Business Update </U></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Global retail sales growth (excluding foreign currency impact) of 5.9% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">U.S. same store sales growth of 1.6% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">International same store sales growth of 1.5% </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Global net store growth of 69 </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center">Diluted EPS up 39.5% to $3.07 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>ANN ARBOR,
Michigan, April</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;23, 2020: Domino&#146;s Pizza, Inc. (NYSE: DPZ),</B> the largest pizza company in the world based on global retail sales, announced results for the first quarter. Global retail sales increased 4.4% in the first
quarter, or 5.9% excluding foreign currency impact. U.S. same store sales grew 1.6% during the quarter versus the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">year-ago</FONT> period, continuing the positive sales momentum in the Company&#146;s U.S. stores
business. The international business also posted positive results, with same store sales growth of 1.5% during the quarter. The first quarter marked the 105<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> consecutive quarter of international
same store sales growth and the 36<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">th</SUP> consecutive quarter of U.S. same store sales growth. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the
quarter, the Company opened 178 gross new stores and 69 net new stores, comprised of 30 net new U.S. stores and 39 net new international stores. The Company&#146;s net store growth includes the closure of its South Africa market, unrelated to the <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">COVID-19</FONT> pandemic, comprising 71 stores in total. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">First quarter diluted EPS was $3.07, up 39.5% over the prior year
quarter. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&nbsp;21, 2020, the Company&#146;s Board of Directors declared a $0.78 per share quarterly dividend for shareholders of record as of
June&nbsp;15, 2020 to be paid on June&nbsp;30, 2020. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In a time of unprecedented change in our industry, I am pleased to report that Domino&#146;s
is in a very strong financial position, both at the brand and franchisee levels,&#148; said Ritch Allison, Domino&#146;s Chief Executive Officer. &#147;We can&#146;t predict the full impact of COVID-19 on the broader economy and we don&#146;t know
how consumer behavior and restaurant purchasing patterns may evolve coming out of this crisis. What I do know is that our franchisees and teams in the U.S. and across the globe will remain focused on safely serving our customers and our communities
in this time of need. I have great confidence in our people and our ability to manage through this crisis, and I remain optimistic about the long-term potential of the Domino&#146;s brand.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>First Quarter Highlights (Unaudited): </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE CELLSPACING="0" CELLPADDING="0" WIDTH="100%" BORDER="0" STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" ALIGN="center">

<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Revenues </B>increased $37.1&nbsp;million, or 4.4%, in the first quarter of 2020. This increase was primarily
due to an increase in global store counts during the trailing four quarters as well as U.S. and international same store sales growth, resulting in higher supply chain and U.S. and international franchise revenues. The increases in revenues were
partially offset by lower U.S. Company-owned store revenues resulting from the previously disclosed sale of 59 U.S. Company-owned stores to certain of the Company&#146;s existing U.S. franchisees during the second quarter of 2019.
</P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="1%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="2%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Net Income</B> increased $29.0&nbsp;million, or 31.2%, in the first quarter of 2020. This increase was
primarily driven by a lower effective tax rate as compared to the prior year quarter as a result of higher tax benefits from equity-based compensation. Higher royalty revenues from U.S. and international franchised stores and higher supply chain
volumes also benefited net income. The increase in net income was partially offset by higher net interest expense as a result of a higher average debt balance. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B>Diluted EPS</B> was $3.07 for the first quarter versus $2.20 in the prior year quarter. This represents a
$0.87, or 39.5%, increase over the prior year quarter. The increase in diluted EPS was driven by higher net income, as well as lower diluted share count, primarily resulting from the Company&#146;s share repurchases during the trailing four
quarters. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>

(409) <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">217-8311</FONT> (International). Ask for the Domino&#146;s Pizza conference call, ID 3263126. The call will also be webcast, and will be archived for one year, on <U>biz.dominos.com</U>. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Company Withdraws Two- to Three-Year Outlook </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Due to the
current uncertainty surrounding the global economy and the Company&#146;s business operations considering&nbsp;COVID-19,&nbsp;the Company is withdrawing its two-to three-year outlook for global retail sales growth, U.S. same store sales growth,
international same store sales growth and global net unit growth. </P>

<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">During the first week of the first quarter of 2020, the Company repurchased and retired 271,064 shares of its common stock in open market repurchases under its
Board of Directors-approved share repurchase program for approximately $79.6&nbsp;million. As of March&nbsp;22, 2020, the Company&#146;s total remaining authorized amount for share repurchases under such program was approximately
$326.6&nbsp;million. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Liquidity </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As of March&nbsp;22,

<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Comments on Regulation G </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">In addition to the GAAP financial measures set forth in this press release, the Company has included <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-GAAP</FONT> financial
measures within the meaning of Regulation G, including free cash flow metrics. The Company has also included metrics such as global retail sales, global retail sales growth, global retail sales growth, excluding foreign currency impact and same
store sales growth, which are commonly used statistical measures in the quick-service restaurant industry that are important to understanding Company performance. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses <B>&#147;Global retail sales&#148;</B> and <B>&#147;</B><B>Retail sales&#148;</B> to refer to total retail sales at Company-owned and
franchise stores. The Company believes retail sales information is useful in analyzing revenues because franchisees pay royalties and advertising fees that are based on a percentage of franchise retail sales. The Company reviews comparable industry
retail sales information to assess business trends and to track the growth of the Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> brand. In addition, supply chain revenues are directly impacted by changes in franchise
retail sales. Retail sales for franchise stores are reported to the Company by its franchisees and are not included in Company revenues. <B>&#147;Global retail sales growth&#148;</B> and <B>&#147;Retail sales growth&#148; </B>are calculated as the
change of U.S.&nbsp;Dollar retail sales against the comparable period of the prior year. <B>&#147;Global retail sales growth, excluding foreign currency impact&#148;</B> and <B>&#147;</B><B>R</B><B>etail sales growth, excluding foreign currency
impact&#148;</B> are calculated as the change of international local currency retail sales against the comparable period of the prior year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company
uses &#147;<B>Same store sales growth</B>,&#148; which is calculated for a given period by including only sales from stores that had sales in the comparable weeks of both years. International same store sales growth is calculated similarly to U.S.
same store sales growth. Changes in international same store sales are reported excluding foreign currency impacts, which reflect changes in international local currency sales. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Company uses <B>&#147;Free cash flow,&#148;</B> which is calculated as net cash provided by operating activities, less capital expenditures, both as
reported under GAAP. The Company believes that the free cash flow measure is important to investors and other interested persons, and that such persons benefit from having a measure which communicates how much cash flow is available for working
capital needs or to be used for repurchasing debt, making acquisitions, repurchasing common stock or paying dividends. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About Domino&#146;s Pizza<SUP
STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP> </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Founded in 1960, Domino&#146;s Pizza is the largest pizza company in the world based on retail
sales, with a significant business in both delivery and carryout pizza. It ranks among the world&#146;s top public restaurant brands with a global enterprise of more than 17,000 stores in over 90 markets. Domino&#146;s had global retail sales of
over $14.3&nbsp;billion in 2019, with over $7.0&nbsp;billion in the U.S. and nearly $7.3&nbsp;billion internationally. In the first quarter of 2020, Domino&#146;s had global retail sales of over $3.4&nbsp;billion, with over $1.7&nbsp;billion in the
U.S. and over $1.7&nbsp;billion internationally. Its system is comprised of independent franchise owners who accounted for 98% of Domino&#146;s stores as of the end of the first quarter of 2020. Emphasis on technology innovation helped Domino&#146;s
achieve more than half of all global retail sales in 2019 from digital channels, primarily online ordering and mobile applications. In the U.S., Domino&#146;s generates over 65% of sales via digital channels and has developed several innovative
ordering platforms, including those developed for Google Home, Facebook Messenger, Apple Watch, Amazon Echo and Twitter &#150; as well as Domino&#146;s Hotspots<SUP STYLE="font-size:85%; vertical-align:top">&reg;</SUP>, an ordering platform
featuring over 200,000 unique, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-traditional</FONT> delivery locations. In June 2019, through an announced partnership with Nuro, Domino&#146;s furthered its exploration and testing of autonomous pizza delivery. In
late 2019, Domino&#146;s opened the Domino&#146;s Innovation Garage adjacent to its headquarters in Ann Arbor, Michigan to fuel continued technology and operational innovation &#150; while also launching its GPS technology, allowing customers to
follow the progress of the delivery driver from store to doorstep. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Order &#150; <U>dominos.com</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">AnyWare Ordering &#150; <U>anyware.dominos.com</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Company Info
&#150; <U>biz.dominos.com</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Twitter &#150; <U>twitter.com/dominos</U> </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Facebook &#150; <U>facebook.com/dominos</U> </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Instagram &#150;
